-- SOURCE URL: `https://agda.github.io/cubical/Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Equiv.html` {-# OPTIONS --erased-cubical --safe --no-sized-types --no-guardedness #-} module Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Equiv where open import Agda.Primitive open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma open import Agda.Primitive.Cubical renaming (primINeg to ~_; primIMax to _ÔłĘ_; primIMin to _Ôłž_; primHComp to hcomp; primTransp to transp; primComp to comp; itIsOne to 1=1) open import Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path open import Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Sub renaming (Sub to _[_ÔćŽ_]) import Agda.Builtin.Cubical.HCompU as HCompU module Helpers = HCompU.Helpers open Helpers -- We make this a record so that isEquiv can be proved using -- copatterns. This is good because copatterns don't get unfolded -- unless a projection is applied so it should be more efficient. record isEquiv {Ôäô Ôäô'} {A : Set Ôäô} {B : Set Ôäô'} (f : A Ôćĺ B) : Set (Ôäô ÔŐö Ôäô') where no-eta-equality field equiv-proof : (y : B) Ôćĺ isContr (fiber f y) open isEquiv public infix 4 _Ôëâ_ _Ôëâ_ : ÔłÇ {Ôäô Ôäô'} (A : Set Ôäô) (B : Set Ôäô') Ôćĺ Set (Ôäô ÔŐö Ôäô') A Ôëâ B = ╬ú (A Ôćĺ B) \ f Ôćĺ (isEquiv f) equivFun : ÔłÇ {Ôäô Ôäô'} {A : Set Ôäô} {B : Set Ôäô'} Ôćĺ A Ôëâ B Ôćĺ A Ôćĺ B equivFun e = fst e -- Improved version of equivProof compared to Lemma 5 in CCHM. We put -- the (¤ć = i0) face in contr' making it be definitionally c in this -- case. This makes the computational behavior better, in particular -- for transp in Glue. equivProof : ÔłÇ {la lt} (T : Set la) (A : Set lt) Ôćĺ (w : T Ôëâ A) Ôćĺ (a : A) Ôćĺ ÔłÇ ¤ł (f : Partial ¤ł (fiber (w .fst) a)) Ôćĺ fiber (w .fst) a [ ¤ł ÔćŽ f ] equivProof A B w a ¤ł fb = inS (contr' {A = fiber (w .fst) a} (w .snd .equiv-proof a) ¤ł fb) where contr' : ÔłÇ {Ôäô} {A : Set Ôäô} Ôćĺ isContr A Ôćĺ (¤ć : I) Ôćĺ (u : Partial ¤ć A) Ôćĺ A contr' {A = A} (c , p) ¤ć u = hcomp (╬╗ i Ôćĺ ╬╗ { (¤ć = i1) Ôćĺ p (u 1=1) i ; (¤ć = i0) Ôćĺ c }) c {-# BUILTIN EQUIV _Ôëâ_ #-} {-# BUILTIN EQUIVFUN equivFun #-} {-# BUILTIN EQUIVPROOF equivProof #-} module _ {Ôäô : I Ôćĺ Level} (P : (i : I) Ôćĺ Set (Ôäô i)) where private E : (i : I) Ôćĺ Set (Ôäô i) E = ╬╗ i Ôćĺ P i ~E : (i : I) Ôćĺ Set (Ôäô (~ i)) ~E = ╬╗ i Ôćĺ P (~ i) A = P i0 B = P i1 f : A Ôćĺ B f x = transp E i0 x g : B Ôćĺ A g y = transp ~E i0 y u : ÔłÇ i Ôćĺ A Ôćĺ E i u i x = transp (╬╗ j Ôćĺ E (i Ôłž j)) (~ i) x v : ÔłÇ i Ôćĺ B Ôćĺ E i v i y = transp (╬╗ j Ôćĺ ~E ( ~ i Ôłž j)) i y fiberPath : (y : B) Ôćĺ (x╬▓0 x╬▓1 : fiber f y) Ôćĺ x╬▓0 Ôëí x╬▓1 fiberPath y (x0 , ╬▓0) (x1 , ╬▓1) k = ¤ë , ╬╗ j Ôćĺ ╬┤ (~ j) where module _ (j : I) where private sys : A Ôćĺ ÔłÇ i Ôćĺ PartialP (~ j ÔłĘ j) (╬╗ _ Ôćĺ E (~ i)) sys x i (j = i0) = v (~ i) y sys x i (j = i1) = u (~ i) x ¤ë0 = comp ~E (sys x0) ((╬▓0 (~ j))) ¤ë1 = comp ~E (sys x1) ((╬▓1 (~ j))) ╬Ş0 = fill ~E (sys x0) (inS (╬▓0 (~ j))) ╬Ş1 = fill ~E (sys x1) (inS (╬▓1 (~ j))) sys = ╬╗ {j (k = i0) Ôćĺ ¤ë0 j ; See end of file for an example. -} {-# OPTIONS --no-exact-split #-} module Cubical.Displayed.Record where open import Cubical.Foundations.Prelude open import Cubical.Foundations.Function open import Cubical.Foundations.Equiv open import Cubical.Foundations.Isomorphism open import Cubical.Foundations.Path open import Cubical.Data.Sigma open import Cubical.Data.List as List open import Cubical.Data.Unit open import Cubical.Data.Bool open import Cubical.Data.Maybe as Maybe open import Cubical.Displayed.Base open import Cubical.Displayed.Properties open import Cubical.Displayed.Prop open import Cubical.Displayed.Sigma open import Cubical.Displayed.Unit open import Cubical.Displayed.Universe open import Cubical.Displayed.Auto import Agda.Builtin.Reflection as R open import Cubical.Reflection.Base import Cubical.Reflection.RecordEquiv as RE {- `DUAFields` A collection of DURG characterizations for fields of a record is described by an element of this inductive family. If you just want to see how to use it, have a look at the end of the file first. An element of `DUAFields ­Łĺ«-A R _ÔëůRÔčĘ_Ôčę_ ¤ÇS ­Łĺ«ß┤░-S ¤ÇSÔëů` describes a mapping - from a structure `R : A Ôćĺ Type _` and notion of structured equivalence `_ÔëůRÔčĘ_Ôčę_`, which are meant to be defined as parameterized record types, - to a DURG `­Łĺ«ß┤░-S`, the underlying structure of which will be an iterated ╬ú-type, - via projections `¤ÇS` and `¤ÇSÔëů`. `­Łĺ«-A`, `R`, and `_ÔëůRÔčĘ_Ôčę_` are parameters, while `¤ÇS`, `­Łĺ«ß┤░-S`, and `¤ÇSÔëů` are indices; the user builds up the ╬ú-type representation of the record using the DUAFields constructors. A DUAFields representation is _total_ when the projections `¤ÇS` and `¤ÇSÔëů` are equivalences, in which case we obtain a DURG on `R` with `_ÔëůRÔčĘ_Ôčę_` as the notion of structured equivalence---see `­Łĺ«ß┤░-Fields` below. When `R`, and `_ÔëůRÔčĘ_Ôčę_` are defined by record types, we can use reflection to automatically generate proofs `¤ÇS` and `¤ÇSÔëů` are equivalences---see `­Łĺ«ß┤░-Record` below. -} data DUAFields {ÔäôA ÔäôÔëůA ÔäôR ÔäôÔëůR} {A : Type ÔäôA} (­Łĺ«-A : UARel A ÔäôÔëůA) (R : A Ôćĺ Type ÔäôR) (_ÔëůRÔčĘ_Ôčę_ : {a a' : A} Ôćĺ R a Ôćĺ UARel._Ôëů_ ­Łĺ«-A a a' Ôćĺ R a' Ôćĺ Type ÔäôÔëůR) : ÔłÇ {ÔäôS ÔäôÔëůS} {S : A Ôćĺ Type ÔäôS} (¤ÇS : ÔłÇ {a} Ôćĺ R a Ôćĺ S a) (­Łĺ«ß┤░-S : DUARel ­Łĺ«-A S ÔäôÔëůS) (¤ÇSÔëů : ÔłÇ {a} {r : R a} {e} {r' : R a} Ôćĺ r ÔëůRÔčĘ e Ôčę r' Ôćĺ DUARel._Ôëůß┤░ÔčĘ_Ôčę_ ­Łĺ«ß┤░-S (¤ÇS r) e (¤ÇS r')) Ôćĺ Type¤ë where -- `fields:` -- Base case, no fields yet recorded in `­Łĺ«ß┤░-S`. fields: : DUAFields ­Łĺ«-A R _ÔëůRÔčĘ_Ôčę_ (╬╗ _ Ôćĺ tt) (­Łĺ«ß┤░-Unit ­Łĺ«-A) (╬╗ _ Ôćĺ tt) -- `ÔÇŽ data[ ¤ÇF Ôłú ­Łĺ«ß┤░-F Ôłú ¤ÇFÔëů ]` -- Add a new field with a DURG. `¤ÇF` should be the name of the field in the structure record `R` and `¤ÇFÔëů` -- the name of the corresponding field in the equivalence record `_ÔëůRÔčĘ_Ôčę_`, while `­Łĺ«ß┤░-F` is a DURG for the -- field's type over `­Łĺ«-A`. -- SOURCE URL: `https://agda.github.io/cubical/Cubical.Foundations.Equiv.html` {- Theory about equivalences Definitions are in Core/Glue.agda but re-exported by this module - isEquiv is a proposition ([isPropIsEquiv]) - Any isomorphism is an equivalence ([isoToEquiv]) There are more statements about equivalences in Equiv/Properties.agda: - if f is an equivalence then (cong f) is an equivalence - if f is an equivalence then precomposition with f is an equivalence - if f is an equivalence then postcomposition with f is an equivalence -} module Cubical.Foundations.Equiv where open import Cubical.Foundations.Function open import Cubical.Foundations.Prelude open import Cubical.Foundations.Isomorphism open import Cubical.Foundations.Equiv.Base public open import Cubical.Data.Sigma.Base private variable Ôäô Ôäô' Ôäô'' : Level A B C D : Type Ôäô infixr 30 _ÔłÖÔéĹ_ equivIsEquiv : (e : A Ôëâ B) Ôćĺ isEquiv (equivFun e) equivIsEquiv e = snd e equivCtr : (e : A Ôëâ B) (y : B) Ôćĺ fiber (equivFun e) y equivCtr e y = e .snd .equiv-proof y .fst equivCtrPath : (e : A Ôëâ B) (y : B) Ôćĺ (v : fiber (equivFun e) y) Ôćĺ Path _ (equivCtr e y) v equivCtrPath e y = e .snd .equiv-proof y .snd -- Proof using isPropIsContr. Here we demand something much stronger, namely that we are given automorphisms that carry the base point to any given point y. If in addition we require this automorphism to be the identity for the base point, then we recover the notion of a left-invertible H-space, and indeed, any homogeneous type in our sense gives rise to such, as shown in: Cubical.Homotopy.HSpace -} isHomogeneous : ÔłÇ {Ôäô} Ôćĺ Pointed Ôäô Ôćĺ Type (Ôäô-suc Ôäô) isHomogeneous {Ôäô} (A , x) = ÔłÇ y Ôćĺ Path (Pointed Ôäô) (A , x) (A , y) -- Pointed -- SOURCE URL: `https://agda.github.io/cubical/Cubical.Foundations.Univalence.Dependent.html` {- Dependent Version of Univalence The univalence corresponds to the dependent equivalences/isomorphisms, c.f. `Cubical.Foundations.Equiv.Dependent`. -} module Cubical.Foundations.Univalence.Dependent where open import Cubical.Foundations.Prelude open import Cubical.Foundations.Equiv open import Cubical.Foundations.Equiv.HalfAdjoint open import Cubical.Foundations.Equiv.Dependent open import Cubical.Foundations.Univalence private variable Ôäô Ôäô' : Level -- Dependent Univalence -- -- Given families `P` and `Q` over base types `A` and `B` -- respectively, and given -- * an equivalence of base types `e : A Ôëâ B`, -- * and and a pointwise equivalence of the families, -- construct a dependent path over `ua e` between the families. module _ {A B : Type Ôäô} {P : A Ôćĺ Type Ôäô'} {Q : B Ôćĺ Type Ôäô'} (e : A Ôëâ B) (F : mapOver (e .fst) P Q) (equiv : isEquivOver {P = P} {Q = Q} F) where private -- Bundle `F` and `equiv` into a pointwise equivalence of `P` and `Q`: ╬ô : (a : A) Ôćĺ P a Ôëâ Q (equivFun e a) ╬ô a = F a , equiv a -- A quick proof provided by @ecavallo. -- Unfortunately it gives a larger term overall. _ : PathP (╬╗ i Ôćĺ ua e i Ôćĺ Type Ôäô') P Q _ = uaÔćĺ (╬╗ a Ôćĺ ua (╬ô a)) uaOver : PathP (╬╗ i Ôćĺ ua e i Ôćĺ Type Ôäô') P Q uaOver i x = Glue Base {¤ć} equiv-boundary where -- Like `ua`, `uaOver` is obtained from a line of -- Glue-types, except that they are glued -- over a line dependent on `ua e : A Ôëí B`. -- `x` is a point along the path `A Ôëí B` obtained -- from univalence, i.e. glueing over `B`: -- -- A = = (ua e) = = B -- | | -- (e) (idEquiv B) -- | | -- v v -- B =====(B)====== B _ : Glue B {¤ć = i ÔłĘ ~ i} (╬╗ { (i = i0) Ôćĺ A , e ; (i = i1) Ôćĺ B , idEquiv B }) _ = x -- We can therefore `unglue` it to obtain a term in the base line of `ua e`, -- i.e. term of type `B`: ¤ć = i ÔłĘ ~ i b : B b = unglue ¤ć x -- This gives us a line `(i : I) ÔŐó Base` in the universe of types, -- along which we can glue the equivalences `╬ô x` and `idEquiv (Q x)`: -- -- P (e x) = = = = = = Q x -- | | -- (╬ô x) (idEquiv (Q x)) -- | | -- v v -- Q x ===(Base)=== Q x Base : Type Ôäô' Base = Q b equiv-boundary : Partial ¤ć (╬ú[ T Ôłł Type Ôäô' ] T Ôëâ Base) equiv-boundary (i = i0) = P x , ╬ô x equiv-boundary (i = i1) = Q x , idEquiv (Q x) -- Note that above `(i = i0) ÔŐó x : A` and `(i = i1) ÔŐó x : B`, -- thus `P x` and `Q x` are well-typed. _ : Partial i B _ = ╬╗ { (i = i1) Ôćĺ x } _ : Partial (~ i) A _ = ╬╗ { (i = i0) Ôćĺ x } -- Dependent `isoToPath` open isHAEquiv isoToPathOver : {A B : Type Ôäô} {P : A Ôćĺ Type Ôäô'} {Q : B Ôćĺ Type Ôäô'} (f : A Ôćĺ B) (hae : isHAEquiv f) (isom : IsoOver (isHAEquivÔćĺIso hae) P Q) Ôćĺ PathP (╬╗ i Ôćĺ ua (_ , isHAEquivÔćĺisEquiv hae) i Ôćĺ Type Ôäô') P Q isoToPathOver f hae isom = uaOver _ _ (isoToEquivOver f hae isom)

-- SOURCE URL: `https://agda.github.io/cubical/Cubical.HITs.James.Inductive.Reduced.html` {- This file contains: - Some alternative inductive definitions of James, and they give the same results. The most relevant one is called `­ŁĽüRed` because it is much simpler. It has fewer constructors, among which the 2-dimensional constructor `coh` has a form essentially more clearer, and it avoids indexes. -} module Cubical.HITs.James.Inductive.Reduced where open import a monoid in "homotopy category". - The equivalence "James XÔéŐ Ôëâ List X" for type X, where XÔéŐ denotes the type formed by freely adjoining a base point to X. -} module Cubical.HITs.James.Properties
